  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_e2d668a4-7217-4e06-83a4-f89b6fcb3f18'
      });
    }

      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer834960880" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3308018855213660502"><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1392128053ra/8504570.gif' alt=' photo uhmmmno_zps0c691a5a.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>2.5 stars ... maybe 2.75 at best<br/><br/>2 for the actual book that was really <i>just</i> 'ok' (IMO) and .5/.75 for the author trying to remain a 'mystery' and all that jazz.<br/><br/>I get it, OK? BDSM is all the rage right now and male POV IS very popular with readers so throw out there a concept for a book that has a story told from male POV that is actually <i>written</i> by a man, who, apparently, "enjoyed several years involved in the BDSM lifestyle" and I am sure you'll get the buzz going.<br/><br/>Too bad "enjoying several years</span>
  <span id="freeText3308018855213660502" style="display:none"><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1392128053ra/8504570.gif" alt=" photo uhmmmno_zps0c691a5a.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>2.5 stars ... maybe 2.75 at best<br><br>2 for the actual book that was really <i>just</i> 'ok' (IMO) and .5/.75 for the author trying to remain a 'mystery' and all that jazz.<br><br>I get it, OK? BDSM is all the rage right now and male POV IS very popular with readers so throw out there a concept for a book that has a story told from male POV that is actually <i>written</i> by a man, who, apparently, "enjoyed several years involved in the BDSM lifestyle" and I am sure you'll get the buzz going.<br><br>Too bad "enjoying several years involved in the BDSM lifestyle" doesn't make you a writer.<br><br>You know the saying "likes to hear the sound of his own voice"?? This is what this book feels like. As if this guy wanted to be interviewed by <i>someone</i> so bad and when nobody came knocking said to himself "I'll just write a book about being interviewed" ... Give me a fucking break.<br><br>Three reasons this book didn't work for me:<br><br>The interviewer ... Leticia. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1392126854ra/8504415.gif" alt=" photo ryanrollingeyes_zps968bc419.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I didn't know you can become a reporter with an IQ of a pencil or can you?? What paper would hire someone as stupid as this chick?? 'Daily Prophet'? I am sure even they have stardards. I am curious if the author did that so the male character would appear 'smarter' next to her? What? He didn't think we got that he was brilliant because he threw around Latin terms??<br><br>Quotes like this one:<br><br><i>“I went to the kitchen, found a glass in a cupboard and filled it with tap water. As a rule I never drank the stuff. Fish have sex in water… think about that…”</i><br> <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1392127298ra/8504508.gif" alt=" photo areyoufuckingkiddingme_zps2b4f3271.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>And last but not least, Jonah/Luke or Luke/Jonah. Talk about having a fucking superiority complex. Dude, confidence is sexy. Arrogance is not. Just FYI.<br><br><br><br>See this:<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1392128366ra/8504608.gif" alt=" photo gymathomecalledthebedroom_zps8bc157b4.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I would rather watch Phyllis "work out" than recommend this book ... <br><br><br><br>P.S. Thank you, M, for lending me a copy.</span>

What can I say?! First off it's written by a guy, um, hello, a guy!!!! That had me from the start right there! This wasn't meant to be a story that was sugar coated, it was to give you a glimpse as to what it is like to be a Master and some of his experiences when he lived that lifestyle while being interviewed.<br><br>I did find it frustrating reading without any chapters.<br><a href="http://s15.photobucket.com/user/Bergyb2424/media/giphy3_zpsdf29c0c9.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1391933044ra/8477574.gif" alt=" photo giphy3_zpsdf29c0c9.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>But I understand why they were left out besides the few breaks in the writing. The flow of the story would have been too interrupted by having actual chapters, plus for readers like me who like stopping at chapters when going to bed it makes us continue reading till we fall asleep because we're so damn tired but just can't STOP reading because it's THAT damn good of a book! <br><br>And then we get to the ending. WTF?!?!?!? Just when I think I have an idea of what might possibly happen next, I'm thrown completely for a curve and the book ends! I think I felt all of these and more and am still trying to figure out exactly how I feel. <br><a href="http://s15.photobucket.com/user/Bergyb2424/media/giphy1_zpsbd56187c.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/845996146?book_show_action=true">Feb 05, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Michelle" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Michelle" href="/user/show/10367112-michelle">Michelle</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10367112-michelle?shelf=arc">arc</a>,

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10367112-michelle?shelf=erotica">erotica</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10367112-michelle?shelf=adult-fiction">adult-fiction</a>,

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10367112-michelle?shelf=master-sub-relationship">master-sub-relationship</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer845996146" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3388738819839785902"><i> *ARC provided by author in exchange for honest review*</i><br/><br/><b>****4.5 I want more Jonah Noble stars****</b><br/><br/><a href='http://www.flickr.com/photos/66034700@N08/12367520985/' title='Master7 by ms.meesh, on Flickr' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1391799041i/8458961.jpg' width='384' height='500' alt='Master7' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>Interview With A Master by Jason Luke took me by surprise. It is truly an interview like no other. Mr. Luke informs his readers that he had spent and enjoyed several years in the BDSM lifestyle so this book is based on several real-life encounters and of fiction He will not state which parts are autobiographical. Interview with a Master focuses on Jonah Noble and his tale of how he became of a Mas</span>
  <span id="freeText3388738819839785902" style="display:none"><i> *ARC provided by author in exchange for honest review*</i><br><br><b>****4.5 I want more Jonah Noble stars****</b><br><br><a href="http://www.flickr.com/photos/66034700@N08/12367520985/" title="Master7 by ms.meesh, on Flickr" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1391799041i/8458961.jpg" width="384" height="500" alt="Master7" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Interview With A Master by Jason Luke took me by surprise. It is truly an interview like no other. Mr. Luke informs his readers that he had spent and enjoyed several years in the BDSM lifestyle so this book is based on several real-life encounters and of fiction He will not state which parts are autobiographical. Interview with a Master focuses on Jonah Noble and his tale of how he became of a Master in the BDSM world. <br><br><a href="http://www.flickr.com/photos/66034700@N08/12359595604/" title="master3 by ms.meesh, on Flickr" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1391760711i/8451187.jpg" width="333" height="500" alt="master3" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>"Jonah Noble at age nineteen was a self-obsessed bastard. Jonah Noble at age twenty-five was still learning to understand women, and certainly not a worthy Master. It's only now- fifteen years after I first met Claire-that I consider myself a decent man."</b><br><br><a href="http://www.flickr.com/photos/66034700@N08/12359216873/" title="mastercollage by ms.meesh, on Flickr" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1391760153i/8451139.jpg" width="500" height="375" alt="mastercollage" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>When newspaper intern, Leticia first appeared to interview Jonah Noble, a Master in BDSM, she did not expect her interview would take on the course it did. As the two spend more time together, it developed into more of a deeper friendship. This is no ordinary tale of woman meets man and falls in <i>love</i> but simply a man and woman getting to know each other to the point that there is this <i>real desire</i> for each other. Jonah’s story-telling of his life will have readers anticipating what’s next and holding their breath as was in the case for Leticia . <br><br><b>"More than that, generally speaking, in a BDSM relationship, the submissive is the one who holds the real power. Because BDSM is based on consent. The Master cannot exert control and power over someone who does not willingly- willingly offer themselves. A Master without a submissive is a guy. Just a guy. He needs someone who wishes to submit to him, in order to become a Master."</b> ~Jonah<br><br><a href="http://www.flickr.com/photos/66034700@N08/12367317485/" title="master6 by ms.meesh, on Flickr" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1391794865i/8458326.jpg" width="500" height="375" alt="master6" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>What truly makes Interview with a Master stand out is that not only it is told in Jonah’s point of view but rather the way he tells his story. Jonah does not give you a standard interview of what people expects or interprets of what the BDSM lifestyle consist of. He gives Leticia an interview of a lifetime with raw, honest, and straight to the point. He doesn’t give you bullshit answers but the TRUTH!! The straightforwardness of his answers in the interview will truly capture your attention and will want you to know more of Jonah Noble. Personally speaking, I found reading a man’s point of view on the BDSM lifestyle more interesting. <br><br><a href="http://www.flickr.com/photos/66034700@N08/12358408245/" title="Master1 by ms.meesh, on Flickr" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1391756986i/8450299.jpg" width="500" height="452" alt="Master1" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><a href="http://www.flickr.com/photos/66034700@N08/12366970823/" title="Fotor020785919 by ms.meesh, on Flickr" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1391792932i/8457981.jpg" width="500" height="375" alt="Fotor020785919" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>The way Mr. Luke was able to capture Jonah and tells his story was done so beautifully. I wouldn’t say this is your typical traditional erotica BDSM book. So if you are looking for a red room of pain, well don’t. There is none. This book is about Master Jonah and his rules. His rules of what a Dom/Sub relationship is like. His rules of punishment. His rules and the way he likes to do it. At the end of the book, I was left holding my breath and wanted more of Jonah Noble. I did not want the interview to end. If you are expecting a happily ever after, there is none. Mr. Luke will leave you shock at the end and have you screaming at your kindle, WHY!! So, I am hoping that there will be a book 2 and Mr. Luke will continue the beautiful development of Jonah and Leticia. <br><br><a href="http://www.flickr.com/photos/66034700@N08/12367217133/" title="master4 by ms.meesh, on Flickr" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1391793847i/8458251.jpg" width="500" height="500" alt="master4" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>"Every man should make the effort occasionally to throw the rule book out. It doesn't matter if the relationship is BDSM or vanilla- every man should go out of his way to make the woman in his world feel desired and wanted. It's worth the effort and planning to occasionally appear spontaneous." </b>~Jonah<br><br><a href="http://www.flickr.com/photos/66034700@N08/12367819155/" title="Fotor0207100234 by ms.meesh, on Flickr" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1391796842i/8458603.jpg" width="500" height="375" alt="Fotor0207100234" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><i>**Reviews on Behalf of Give Me Books Blog**</i><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/7776521.Jason_Luke" title="Jason Luke" rel="nofollow noopener">Jason Luke</a></span>

The art of seduction and the mastery of claiming a woman’s trust. This is his story, told through his experi</span>
  <span id="freeText12886219054103217830" style="display:none"><b>4.5 anticipating stars</b><br><br>Jason Luke’s Interview with a Master takes you on a journey like no other. Reality and fantasy mingle as his story is told, through the voice of Jonah Noble. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1391893944i/8472426.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>Jonah Noble is a businessman, he’s wealthy and he is Master. Ready to tell his story to the world. What led him to this lifestyle, what kept him so wrapped up in the idea of a woman’s submission that he stayed. The art of seduction and the mastery of claiming a woman’s trust. This is his story, told through his experiences.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1391893944i/8472427.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>Leticia Fall has never fantasized too much about the idea of BDSM, but as she interviews Jonah she finds herself more and more aroused by the idea. Leaving the dull gray of a small town to live her life in color; Leticia finds herself on the cusp of a career making situation. Jonah may be newsworthy in his business life, but his private life has never been exposed in such vivid details. He wants his full story to be told and he wants her to be the one to tell it.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1391893944i/8472428.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>When I started to see the teasers for this story I knew this was going to be a drop-everything-and-read-it-now book. The concept of this story was fresh and the fact that some parts were based the author’s experience was intriguing in its own way. But this story was all about anticipation for me. Not just of what he was going to reveal, but where they were going to go. Jason Luke did a fantastic job of ensuring that you were always craving more. More of Jonah’s stories – more of his questions of Leticia – more of just.... <i>everything. </i><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1391894219i/8472473.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Although I knew there was no way I was not going to read this book immediately, I was not quite sure if the format of the story would work for me. I was pleasantly surprised to find that I was still able to be fully enraptured by, not only the revelations of his past, the insight into a woman’s mind and her body, but the slow dance of the attraction of these two. The way his stories exposed her desires, the slow stoking of the flames of the unknown. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1391894219i/8472474._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>After finishing this there is just one thing that I want... <i>more.</i> <br><br>With the recounting of events and erotic experiences, I found that the exposure of his life and her reactions far more enticing than the actual scenes laid out. It was as if we were slowly being seduced by his words. <br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b> “I want you – and I need you, but I don’t want you to fall in love with me.” <br>“What makes you so sure that I will?” <br>I smiled, but there was no humor. <br>“Because I’m fighting with all my strength to stop falling in love with you.” </b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1391894219i/8472475.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>This felt like a slow tease, building up to the conclusion of the story but leaving so much left unsaid. The story could easily end here, but I can’t help but want see this story continue. If you are a fan of erotica and love something that is not just the same story retold with new characters, this is <b>your</b> book. <br></span>
  <a data-text-id="12886219054103217830" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/835443669" />
    <a title="Lucia" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/8837962-lucia"><img alt="Lucia" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1484242793p2/8837962.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/835443669?book_show_action=true">Jan 26, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Lucia" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Lucia" href="/user/show/8837962-lucia">Lucia</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8837962-lucia?shelf=1-2-stars-read">1-2-stars-read</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer835443669" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2217629409799514227">My Jonah and Leticia:<br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1391983364i/8483802._SX540_.jpg' width='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><i>When presented with a chance of scoring exclusive interview with "America's elusive, notorious BDSM Master, Jonah Noble", Leticia Falls doesn't hesitate. But while Jonah shares his story, relives his past sexual encounters and explains his lifestyle; he wants something in return from Leticia...</i><br/><br/>If Interview with a Master was supposed to be a sexy story, author definitely failed somewhere. I expected to be seduced, entertained and immersed in the world of Master Jonah. Unfortu</span>
  <span id="freeText2217629409799514227" style="display:none">My Jonah and Leticia:<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1391983364i/8483802._SX540_.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>When presented with a chance of scoring exclusive interview with "America's elusive, notorious BDSM Master, Jonah Noble", Leticia Falls doesn't hesitate. But while Jonah shares his story, relives his past sexual encounters and explains his lifestyle; he wants something in return from Leticia...</i><br><br>If Interview with a Master was supposed to be a sexy story, author definitely failed somewhere. I expected to be seduced, entertained and immersed in the world of Master Jonah. Unfortunatelly, I wasn't any of those things. Writing had this terse forced vibe and many things that Jonah said were <b>turning me off</b> instead of being hot. I get it that a Master has to be dominating. But Jonah Noble was crass (not in a sexy aplha male way), did some disturbing things and overall didn't fit into my image of attractive and charismatic narrator of erotic novel.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1391983364i/8483803.png" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I have to admit that I picked this book mainly because it is supposed to be written by a man who participates in BDSM lifestyle. Prior to reading this book I wasn't sure if I should believe it or if it was only a part of marketing. But now, after reading this story myself, I would say it is a true. It was clear that narrator was very passionate about subject matter. However, author's <b>storytelling skills</b> were slightly <b>amateurish</b> and all over the place. And while it is understandable when it comes to debut novel of new author, it doesn't mean that I have to like it or that readers should ignore it.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1391983364i/8483804._SY540_.png" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>At first, I thought that author's attempt to write this book in interview-like style is interesting and appealing idea. But it didn't work for me in reality.<br><br>Firstly, story missed addictive feeling I have when reading classical novel and it <b>never hold my comeplete attention</b>. If it was a result of untraditional format of storyline or story itself, I cannot tell. But result was the same - I lacked the connection with characters.<br><br>Secondly, author did a poor job of separating Jonah's past and present feelings. While recollecting with a big pleasure his thoughts and feelings towards his past sexual partners, Jonah simultaneously thought intimately about Leticia. It made <b>Leticia look like sexual object</b>, rather than a woman he was interested in and I never felt real believable attraction between Leticia and Jonah. It seemed like author put too much on his plate. Explaining BDSM, telling how Jonah became who he is now and depicting rising attraction between Jonah and Leticia. All at once. And it all blew up in his face.<br><br><b>I am sure that this book has its target group and that it will be loved by many. However, I was not impressed by this story and found it rather disappointing.</b> <br><br>MORE REVIEWS ON MY BLOG <a href="http://readingismybreathing.blogspot.cz/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <b>Reading Is My Breathing</b>
</a><br><br></span>

    <a title="~ Becs ~" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2626261-becs"><img alt="~ Becs ~" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1388693144p2/2626261.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/849635670?book_show_action=true">Feb 09, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="~ Becs ~" class="user" itemprop="url" name="~ Becs ~" href="/user/show/2626261-becs">~ Becs ~</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2626261-becs?shelf=kindle">kindle</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2626261-becs?shelf=bdsm-kink">bdsm-kink</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2626261-becs?shelf=super-rich-hero">super-rich-hero</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2626261-becs?shelf=smuttastic">smuttastic</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2626261-becs?shelf=erotic-romance">erotic-romance</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer849635670" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10708363182926891002"><p>
  <em>Click </em>
  <a href='http://sinfullysexybooks.blogspot.co.uk/2014/02/interview-with-master-review-author.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
    <em>here</em>
  </a>
  <em> to read an interview with Jason Luke and enter to win a copy of Interview With A Master.</em>
</p><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1392228433i/8521966._SX540_.jpg' alt=' photo interviewwithamasterquotey_zpsd4eb7685.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>This one really jumped out of nowhere for me. Last week, I’d never even heard of Jason Luke and now I’m a huge fan and I’ve even interviewed him. Interview With A Master is the story of one dominant, Jonah Noble, telling his story over several days to a journalist intern, Leticia Fall. After she asks him several superficial questions, Jonah demands that she conducts a ‘proper’ int</span>
  <span id="freeText10708363182926891002" style="display:none"><p>
  <em>Click </em>
  <a href="http://sinfullysexybooks.blogspot.co.uk/2014/02/interview-with-master-review-author.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
    <em>here</em>
  </a>
  <em> to read an interview with Jason Luke and enter to win a copy of Interview With A Master.</em>
</p><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1392228433i/8521966._SX540_.jpg" alt=" photo interviewwithamasterquotey_zpsd4eb7685.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>This one really jumped out of nowhere for me. Last week, I’d never even heard of Jason Luke and now I’m a huge fan and I’ve even interviewed him. Interview With A Master is the story of one dominant, Jonah Noble, telling his story over several days to a journalist intern, Leticia Fall. After she asks him several superficial questions, Jonah demands that she conducts a ‘proper’ interview and offers her a career-making interview with America’s elusive, notorious BDSM Master.<br><br>And so we begin. And from this moment I was completely captivated, utterly enthralled as I listened to that intoxicating voice telling his story. We chart his metamorphosis from horny teenage virgin to the calm, collected and very commanding dominant we see before us today and I was hooked and just about ready to kneel at his feet.<br><br>Not one to allow just one way traffic, Jonah insists that, for every revelation he gives Leticia, she reciprocates with one equally as personal about herself.<br><br><blockquote>I smiled thinly and shook my head. “Not yet.‘Do ut des’, Leticia.”<br><br>She frowned.<br><br>“It’s a Latin term,” I explained. “It means ‘I give that you may give’. It’s your turn to answer my questions about you. That was the agreement, yes? Our deal is based on the principle of reciprocity.”</blockquote><br><br>What follows is an intoxicating and highly addictive exploration of BDSM with Jonah’s story mostly told in retrospect as his fascination with his interviewer, Leticia, grows stronger as the book progresses but there’s one question he won’t answer and you will have to wait until almost the very end of the book to find out what that is. I’ve seen some criticism of the ending of the book, but for me it’s a brave decision by the author and one that I applaud.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1392228433i/8521967._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo masterjonahquotalicious_zpsea8f1279.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I so enjoyed this sensual novel – I guess what makes it so different is that it’s BDSM told from the male POV by a male author. That’s not something that we see very often but it’s a fascinating insight. I was completely lost, desperate to keep turning those pages to know what was going to happen next, sadly watching the progress indicator on my Kindle creep ever close to 100%, knowing it was all about to end and I just wasn’t ready to part from Jonah. I did think there were a lot of loose ends very close to the finish and wondered if it would all come together by the conclusion but it did and its really quite a shocking ending that took me by surprise, even though the clues were there, and had me gasping in shock.<br><br><blockquote>“More than that, generally speaking, in a BDSM relationship, the submissive is the one who holds the real power.”<br><br>Leticia shook her head. “How can that be?”<br><br>“Because BDSM is based on consent,” I said. “The Master cannot exert control and power over someone who does not willingly –” I raised my finger to emphasize the point, “willingly offer themselves. A Master without a submissive is a guy. Just a guy. He needs someone who wishes to submit to him, in order to become a Master.”</blockquote><br><br>This is a very frank and deliciously hot account of Jonah’s sexual proclivities. It’s eerily atmospheric and the style is fairly reminiscent of Anne Rice’s Interview With The Vampire – I definitely got the same slightly haunting feeling reading this although, of course, the subject matter is very different. Yes, this is highly titillating but it also reads like literary BDSM – it’s a thinkin’ gal’s piece of erotica. It goes deeper than just the physical as Jonah talks at length about the psychological balance between a dom and his sub and I found myself falling for him and was a lost cause by the end of the book. he’s a delicious dominant and yet I found him to be really quite a lonely figure and I felt sad for him. Despite being a man who seemingly has everything and a collection of submissives at his beck and call, he’s lacking that real connection that a true couple shares and I so wanted this for him.<br><br>So this is a highly engaging, utterly compelling and thoughtful piece of fiction and I’m going to name this one a Sinfully Sexy Recommended Read<br><br>5 sensual stars<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1392228433i/8521968._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo masterjonahquotey_zps776c77cc.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><p><a href="http://sinfullysexybooks.blogspot.co.uk/2014/02/interview-with-master-review-author.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">Read this review at Sinfully Sexy</a> | <a href="https://www.facebook.com/sinfullysexybookreviews" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">Follow us on Facebook</a> | <a href="https://twitter.com/SinfullySexyB" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">Follow us on Twitter</a></p></span>
  <a data-text-id="10708363182926891002" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/22115857-shurrn?shelf=z-own-for-kindle">z-own-for-kindle</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer850114574" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5823194242304826826"><b>Mixed feelings for the hotly anticipated Master and his tales of Erotic Exploits disguised as an interview/self-help seminar...</b><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1392148065ra/8508116.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>I was drawn to this book because word on the street (and by "street" I mean GoodReads bookclubs) was that the author was experienced in the BDSM lifestyle and would be offering a new perspective... Other than the fact that this was a MALE perspective, I'm not sure how successful this book was in living up to the hype. <b>It was enjoyable</b>... If you're hoping to read some BDS</span>
  <span id="freeText5823194242304826826" style="display:none"><b>Mixed feelings for the hotly anticipated Master and his tales of Erotic Exploits disguised as an interview/self-help seminar...</b><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1392148065ra/8508116.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I was drawn to this book because word on the street (and by "street" I mean GoodReads bookclubs) was that the author was experienced in the BDSM lifestyle and would be offering a new perspective... Other than the fact that this was a MALE perspective, I'm not sure how successful this book was in living up to the hype. <b>It was enjoyable</b>... If you're hoping to read some BDSM-themed erotica from a male perspective, I say go for it... The whole "interview inside a narrative" structure was entertaining and refreshing for this genre... But it wasn't groundbreaking by any means. It started off strong and began unraveling mid-book.<br><br><b>This is a 3 1/2 star read for me.<br>It lost half a star for overwhelming arrogance.<br>It lost a whole star for the last 20% of the book.</b><br><br>I was thrilled to do a Buddy Read of this book with the amazing Wendy (<a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/17755575-wendy-sthoughts" rel="nofollow noopener">Wendy'sThoughts</a>). Because my experience with this book was shared with her, I must reference a few of the conversations we had while reading together...<br><br><b>She pointed out that the book was split into two narratives:<br>1. The Erotica / Romancing the reader story line...<br>2. The Philosophical Men's Guide to Women &amp; BDSM...</b><br>I agree completely. This split structure was both a blessing and a curse. It keeps the reader on their toes and a little off balance as we try to figure out what Master Jonah's motives are for allowing this interview and for choosing the intern Leticia as the person to document his life.<br><br><b>Reasons to Read it:</b><br>1. Some lovely erotic exploits<br>2. Jonah's endless opinions - even if you don't agree, he's passionate<br>3. The sinking feeling that this whole thing will end badly<br>4. The humor sprinkled throughout<br>3. The quotable "rule book" of Jonah Noble<br><br><b>JONAH NOBLE</b><br>America's elusive, wealthy, notorious BDSM Master...<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1392135459i/8505799._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"It wasn't about physical domination for me. It still isn't. It’s about that emotional transfer of power: the command and control. That’s what turns me on, Leticia. That’s what I find so addictive about being a Master. I love the power, given to me by the submissive."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote> Jonah is known as a Master of all things. King of his business empire and renowned for his expertise in training submissives.<br><br><b>LETICIA FALL</b><br>Aspiring Journalist, Interviewing Master Noble ...<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1392135459i/8505800._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"If you're right, then what you're about to tell me is the secret to success for the average married man. I'd hate to miss a single word.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote> The price for an exclusive in-depth interview with Jonah is that he will be granted the opportunity to return the favor - question for question, answer for answer - neither party will hold anything back.<br><br>This is where Wendy made a very good point - that this book is part <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/43763.Interview_With_The_Vampire__The_Vampire_Chronicles___1_" title="Interview With The Vampire (The Vampire Chronicles, #1) by Anne Rice" rel="nofollow noopener">Interview With The Vampire</a> &amp; part <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/23807.The_Silence_of_the_Lambs__Hannibal_Lecter___2_" title="The Silence of the Lambs (Hannibal Lecter, #2) by Thomas Harris" rel="nofollow noopener">The Silence of the Lambs</a>:<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1392145471ra/8507750.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>This book parallels <b>Interview with the Vampire</b> with respect to the narrative structure... One man telling his epic history to a complete outsider who finds the stories amazing and nearly beyond belief...<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1392145471ra/8507751.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>The similarrity to <b>Silence of the Lambs</b> is found in the calculating and manipulative hero as well as the <i>"quid pro quo"</i> dynamic of give and take between subject and interviewer...<br><br><b>The rest is an ode to Jonah's male ego.</b><br>He spends the entire interview telling stories which highlight his sexual prowess and attempting to demonstrate his expertise of women.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1392143209i/8507321.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>As Master Jonah tells his tales, we are being seduced by him; obviously manipulated. A man telling his own history has complete control of the facts presented...</b><br><br>Jonah's answers are structured around recalling erotic encounters throughout his life - in vivid detail - which follow his journey in becoming a Master. His anecdotes are often punctuated with his opinions on sex in modern society.<br><br>He has very strong opinions on women in general, and considers himself an expert on female sexuality - This is where many readers will find themselves uncomfortable with the broad generalizations which Jonah presents as fact. He knows he is a politically-incorrect jerk, and if you can recognize this facet of his personality, and not get offended, you will handle him as well as Leticia.<br><br>The reader steps into the role of Leticia as we listen to Master Jonah's stories. We are experiencing these erotic stories at the same time, and since the whole story is from Jonah's point of view, we must assume that Leticia's thoughts mirror our own.<br><br><b>My thoughts on the Ending:</b><br>Click the spoiler at your own risk!<br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1385866991ra/7246774.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I don't think anybody was surprised that Leticia wound up with a crush on the Master... But I was put off by how quickly her character deteriorated after growing attached to him. She was never very interesting to begin with, so the fact that they didn't wind up "together" at the end wasn't so heartbreaking to me.<br><br>The whole "I can't fall in love" stance for a Dominant is such a lame way to go. Trust me, there can be love in BDSM. Jonah's feelings toward Leticia were so ridiculously angsty for someone who had shown so much aloof self-control toward women in the past. The only thing she did to attract him was listen to him talk. How much ego is required for that to happen?<br><br>The entire time I was reading this book I was waiting for the "catch" - Jonah is a calculated man, there must be a good reason he chose to tell his story to Leticia. I was making up all kinds of dark scenarios in my head...<br>In my most twisted prediction I wondered if Jonah made a bet with the owner of Leticia's newspaper that he could lure the shy vanilla girl into being his submissive...<br>So when we discovered that Jonah had a brain tumor and was dying, I was massively disappointed. Not shocked (hello headaches throughout the book) just disappointed that there wasn't a big ending... A better reveal... A more dark and twisted motive behind his choice to tell his story.<br><br>The beginning and middle of this book were so strong, that the ending seemed bland in comparison. Will I read the next book? Who knows... I don't really care if Jonah &amp; Letica hook up, but I'd love to hear more about Jonah's saucy past!<br><br><b>Synopsis of Jonah's entire perspective in GIF form:</b><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1392148065ra/8508117.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1387253053ra/7561045.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1392148065ra/8508118.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1392151909ra/8508752.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1392151909ra/8508753.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1392151909ra/8508754.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1385794603ra/7229620.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br> <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br><b>
  <u>Some of My Favorite Moments:</u>
</b><br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[<br>"Relax? Are you for real? You broke into my apartment."<br>"I own the apartment," I corrected her. "This is just a routine inspection."<br>"Inspection? You son of a bitch. I'm standing here half naked!"<br>"Yes," I said admiringly. "But only half naked. I could have waited..."<br><br>"You're not one of my submissives," I pointed out. "And you're not a business rival."<br>She smiled. "So what does that make me?"<br>I considered the question carefully. I tasted the wine. It was good. He needs someone who wishes to submit to him, in order to become a Master."<br><br>There was a long simmering silence.<br>I was the one who was simmering.<br><br>She looked up into my eyes and her expression was almost pained. "Please," she said softly, with a mischievous glint in her eyes, "please don't use another seafood analogy!"<br><br>"...She started to plead."<br>I looked at Leticia. A submissive needs to have complete trust in her Master. She needs to know she can give her mind and body to him with absolute confidence that he will treat them as a gift, not a right. The rest is just tinsel on the tree. It's all decoration."<br><br>"Sex is a sensory thing for women. Sounds and scents are just as important as the other senses. For men it's ll visual, but women are more complex."<br><br>"It's not the room that commands obedience. It's not the props or the decor. It's not the fear of any piece of equipment that compels a submissive to obey, and nor is it the menace of any threat. It's the man that a woman submits herself to, Leticia. Not the room."<br><br>"Anticipation is more potent than a whip and more compelling than handcuffs. The ability to tease and arouse a woman is a subtle skill few men bother to learn," I said. Fish have sex in water... think about that...<br> <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br>This book does have a cliffhanger ending, and as of the date of this review, there is no information on the upcoming second book...<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379798581i/642736.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>As I mentioned (several times) this was a Buddy Read with Wendy. I encourage you to read <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/850124049" rel="nofollow noopener">her review</a> of this book as well. She's awesome, and I get more enjoyment of of a book when I have the opportunity to read with her.</["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/850124049?book_show_action=true">Feb 09, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Wendy&#39;sThoughts" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Wendy&#39;sThoughts" href="/user/show/17755575-wendy-sthoughts">Wendy&#39;sThoughts</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer850124049" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2656920627599268720">First and Foremost...<br/>Thank you Shurrn for Buddy Reading with me... Always. Anytime, Any Book<br/><br/>4 Star BDSM Master's Philosophy Manual or 3 Star Erotica/Romance<br/><br/>I just finish Interview with a Master and feel as if I have read two books at the same time. This book was written by Jason Luke who clearly states from my understanding, a Master's experience in BDSM. For the sake of this book and review, I am believing this is true. <br/><br/>The title reflects exactly how the story is structured... Jonah Noble is th</span>
  <span id="freeText2656920627599268720" style="display:none">First and Foremost...<br>Thank you Shurrn for Buddy Reading with me... Always. Anytime, Any Book<br><br>4 Star BDSM Master's Philosophy Manual or 3 Star Erotica/Romance<br><br>I just finish Interview with a Master and feel as if I have read two books at the same time. This book was written by Jason Luke who clearly states from my understanding, a Master's experience in BDSM. For the sake of this book and review, I am believing this is true. <br><br>The title reflects exactly how the story is structured... Jonah Noble is the elusive, rich, powerful man in his mid thirty's who everyone wonders about. Many articles have been written about his business success; some have hinted to him being involved in the BDSM lifestyle. He has agreed to be interviewed this time by the local newspaper and they have sent Leticia, a young intern to do it. She is wrapping up the questions, thinking she has covered everything when Jonah, frustrated, lashes out and says how juvenile and immature her interview questions were; she could have just read all of the other articles out there and never wasted his time. Something, however, stops him from allowing her to leave.<br><br>He offers her a real opportunity if she is willing to take it...<br><br>He will tell her everything about being a Master, no question unanswered but it will be an equal situation for her... he will ask her anything and she must answer. Leticia ponders this for a moment as she wants to prove herself to the paper; doing an expose' would be a kudo for her. She accepts.<br><br>Here is where I want to explain my ratings for this book... because there really was in my mind 2 books going on at the same time.<br><br>First, there was the Erotica/Romance book of a powerful man telling tales to young inexperienced woman... who had her epiphany of realizing small town life was not for her.... something was missing. She broke the long term engagement to her high school sweetheart... searching for more ... moved to the big city to become a journalist. She is his audience... willing to listen and take notes about how he got into this life... what led him to it... when did he know he was a Dom.... how does he train....all personal memories... as he tells her very graphic sexual experiences from his life... there is an exchange of feelings between them of sorts... and this would be what I call the erotica/romance aspect.<br><br>This was where there were parts of the book which were hot .... I am telling you scorching, steaming, pulsating, get your BOB battery-ready HOT.<br><br>There was so much telling of Jonah's experiences in minute graphic detail it bordered on almost too much... I said almost....there was very little chemistry, though, between theses two... I just didn't feel it. She desired him and what he offered... he seemed drawn to her sweetness and naivete as fresh and new but overall it wasn't overwhelming. I think she was more turned on by the telling of the tales and wish fulfillment of her fantasies. He seemed very involved in the telling of the tales and remembering the past. It also felt at times like he was seducing or grooming her with these memories ....a constant manipulation of one type of another. <br><br>What was more interesting to me was the other book I ended up reading.....a Philosophical Men's Guide to Women with BDSM Explained. Here we were treated to the rare chance of hearing from a Master; what he thought about the workings of sexuality.... all it means with men and women. How anticipation can be power during times together... how heightening the senses this way can cause amazing results... how giving begets giving in all strong relationships... meaning a person needs to understand submitting is not for the taking only but really for the sharing of giving to each other... <br><br>This part of the book had some strong ideas and I felt the real reason it was written in the first place. The author had serious philosophical concepts he wanted to share... things he felt were worthwhile and the best way to get these messages out... through a book which would reach his target audience.<br>Many of these messages are thoughtful and actually would be excellent required reading for men ... in some instances... others things mentioned by him felt more manipulative or generalizations which I was not of agreement. <br><br>So what are my final thoughts.. well, if you read this with the total mindset of this is an erotic/romance then it was a collection of hot steamy sexual tales and I am not sorry I read it. If you read it for insight from a BDSM Master, it had very interesting concepts; was understandable, educational and worth quoting and sharing with both sexes.<br><br>There is a cliffy... be forewarned .... Master Luke is practicing what he preaches... he is giving us book denial with No permission to read the next one yet... <br>For my full experience reading this... please go to Shurrn's review<br>for an incredible analysis. <br><br><strong>For more reviews, Free E-books and Giveaways</strong> <br><a href="http://starangelsreviews.blogspot.com" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1389570358i/8041008._SX540_.jpg" alt=" photo banner_zps637f7ed8.jpg" width="”400”" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br> </span>

<span id="freeTextContainer17617562598680573210"><i>4 'Yes Master' stars</i><br/><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>Women don’t want to be forced to their knees. They want to be made to feel weak at the knees.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1406848737i/10607057._SY540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/> <br/>Leticia is the young journalist looking for a break and it comes in the form of  America’s elusive, notorious BDSM Master, Jonah Noble.   <span id="freeText17617562598680573210" style="display:none"><i>4 'Yes Master' stars</i><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>Women don’t want to be forced to their knees. They want to be made to feel weak at the knees.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1406848737i/10607057._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br> <br>Leticia is the young journalist looking for a break and it comes in the form of  America’s elusive, notorious BDSM Master, Jonah Noble. An interview of a lifetime not to mention an interview that will make or break her career. It's all about giving and taking. He is as curious about her as she is him, but how much is she really prepared to share with a man who is confident and arrogant enough to bare all ….<br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"A Master without a submissive is a guy. Just a guy . He needs someone who wishes to submit to him, in order to become a Master.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1406849293i/10607177.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Not holding anything back, with no apology or regret, Re-living the path Jonah took to be the Master he is today, making sure that Leticia fully understands what it is he is telling her. Leticia is a virgin in the BDSM world, and as they go through the basic understanding of what it means to be in a BDSM relationship. <br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“Anticipating is expectation,” I said. “It’s the mystery of not knowing, and the heightening of all a woman’s senses. Anticipation draws out the moment so that the moment then becomes exquisite,” I explained. “And it is only something as powerful as anticipation that can elevate an ordinary touch to a breathtaking caress.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1406848737ra/10607059.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Behind the privacy of close doors, as secrets, insight and fantasies are shared, it is hard to keep the heart out of coming to conclusions. As desires are satisfied could one really just walk away??? Sometimes fate plays horrible tricks, making you want something you cannot have, making you wish, making you wonder…<br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“Because I’m fighting with all my strength to stop falling in love with you.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1406849293i/10607178._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Interview with a Master</b> was an insightful erotic read from a self proclaimed Master who is confident, dominant and arrogant. He knows what he wants, pushes the limit and tests his control to see how far he can go. Leticia is a young naïve woman, who comes into the BDSM world as a virgin, coming into the interview with her preconceptions while keeping an open mind. Jonah has a sense of mystery behind him as to why do the interview now, why give people access to your private memoirs. I kind of just jumped right into this read, so I wasn't prepared for the ending it had in store, because it literally left me with my mouth wide open. I need to jump on the second book ASAP. </span>

<div id="review_845934816" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/845934816" />
    <a title="J. McCoy" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/19256454-j-mccoy"><img alt="J. McCoy" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1405971771p2/19256454.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/845934816?book_show_action=true">Feb 05, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="J. McCoy" class="user" itemprop="url" name="J. McCoy" href="/user/show/19256454-j-mccoy">J. McCoy</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer845934816" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6574215934415821719">**Warning -- Spoilers ahead!**<br/><br/>I normally try to write spoiler free reviews, because I hate a story to be spoiled for me. I feel that in order for me to tell you what I had issues with, I’m going to have to spoil some things. Sorry, it’s necessary this time.<br/> <a class='jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction'>(view spoiler)</a><span class='spoilerContainer' style='display: none'>[<br/>I liked this book, I didn’t love it. I felt like I was on the sidelines throughout the story. It's Jonah telling his story, with what I felt was very limited interaction with Leticia. Yes, she’s interviewing him but… other than</span></span>
  <span id="freeText6574215934415821719" style="display:none">**Warning -- Spoilers ahead!**<br /><br />I normally try to write spoiler free reviews, because I hate a story to be spoiled for me. I feel that in order for me to tell you what I had issues with, I’m going to have to spoil some things. Sorry, it’s necessary this time.<br /> <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[<br />I liked this book, I didn’t love it. I felt like I was on the sidelines throughout the story. It's Jonah telling his story, with what I felt was very limited interaction with Leticia. Yes, she’s interviewing him but… other than when he asks her questions and they discuss her answers, they don’t get to know each other much. I get that she's turned on by his stories, and he's interested in her because, well, I don't know why, honestly... but for them to kiss once and then declare he's trying to stop himself from falling in love with her just felt out of left field for me. I didn’t connect with Jonah and Leticia as being a couple because there wasn’t enough emotional interaction between them. They did, however, have a ton of sexual chemistry between them. That felt real, it just doesn’t equate falling in love.<br /><br />I felt like the author was trying to use the Interview storyline as a way to give an education in BDSM. Do I know a bunch more about the BDSM lifestyle now, yes. Thank you, Jason Luke, for that. Did some of the stories Jonah told about his past send my heart racing with excitement? Of course, those stories were hot. But, the scenes he was describing to Leticia were very... stiff, and formal. The language he used didn't make it feel like a relaxed interview. Sometimes I felt like things were over described for what he recalling. How could he remember, just exactly, every little thing she did when he touched her and this was supposed to have happened years ago? I can’t remember what I ate for breakfast yesterday.<br /><br />And the ending... She sees him come out of a bedroom and flips out like that? Scratches his face up when they haven't even had sex yet? And then, she just walks away??? The rest of the story didn't equate to that emotional scene for me. The ending twist was too quick to really garner any emotion out of me, and you all know I’m a crier. No tears here people. Not a single one. I really needed more Jonah and Leticia is this story, and less Jonah recalling his previous relationships. I think a whole lot more could have been done with that twist at the end because I didn’t see it coming. I think it just came a little too late.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer2149369940593636288">I received an ARC for an honest review.<br/><br/>I am having a very hard time writing this review because I know it is not easy to write a book and reviews are important but I can not give this book high stars. As I read the other reviews I actually wonder if we read the same book.<br/><br/>The first thing I noticed about this book is that there are no chapters, it like one long story. I had never read a book without chapters but I thought OK and kept reading. I had a VERY hard time finishing this book. <br/><br/>To me there</span>
  <span id="freeText2149369940593636288" style="display:none">I received an ARC for an honest review.<br /><br />I am having a very hard time writing this review because I know it is not easy to write a book and reviews are important but I can not give this book high stars. As I read the other reviews I actually wonder if we read the same book.<br /><br />The first thing I noticed about this book is that there are no chapters, it like one long story. I had never read a book without chapters but I thought OK and kept reading. I had a VERY hard time finishing this book. <br /><br />To me there is no definitive story line, plot twist or even an HEA. The only WTF moment in the book was at 99% and that was predictable, then the story just ends...<br /><br />The sex was hot but all in the past nothing in the present. The more I read this book the more aggravated I got with some of the things he says as a "Master". <br /><br />"Falling in love is the biggest mistake a Master can make" <br /><br />Statements like this through out the book make me wonder if the author really is in the lifestyle because I have never heard that before and I have been in the lifestyle for awhile. <br /><br />I think this story has potential but as it stands right now the only way I would "buy" this book is if it was free...maybe.<br /><br /></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer834338456" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer6564867819547923275"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1392298391i/8534626._SX540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1392298391i/8534627._SY540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Ladies! This is one book that we all need to get our men to read!!<br/><br/><b>3.5 STARS FOR JONAH NOBLE!</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1392298391i/8534628.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1391106540i/8331999.png' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>"Before we go any further, I must warn you that the things I am going to share with you throughout this interview are very explicit. I can either censor the descriptions, or I can tell you in detail. The choice is yours. But if you want the detailed explanation, then you must be prepared for graphic language. I'm no fan of political correctness, so you can't expect me to keep apologizing if your d</b></i></blockquote></span>
  <span id="freeText6564867819547923275" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1392298391i/8534626._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1392298391i/8534627._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Ladies! This is one book that we all need to get our men to read!!<br><br><b>3.5 STARS FOR JONAH NOBLE!</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1392298391i/8534628.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1391106540i/8331999.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">"Before we go any further, I must warn you that the things I am going to share with you throughout this interview are very explicit. I can either censor the descriptions, or I can tell you in detail. The choice is yours. But if you want the detailed explanation, then you must be prepared for graphic language. I'm no fan of political correctness, so you can't expect me to keep apologizing if your delicate, sensitive ears are offended by language."</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1392298391i/8534629.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>So, let's start with the bio on Jason Luke's Goodreads page.<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>Jason Luke enjoyed several years involved in the BDSM lifestyle - but he is quick to point out that his experiences don't qualify him as an expert, any more than knowing how to drive a car makes him a qualified mechanic. 'Interview with a Master' is a novel about how one man became a Master. The book is a work of fiction, but Jason has drawn heavily on encounters from his own real life. He won't say which parts of the book are fictionalised, and which parts are auto-biographical.<br><br>Erotic BDSM fiction written by a man from a man's point of view.</i>
</blockquote><br><br>This fascinated me. I was absolutely gagging for this book after reading that. But, it wasn't quite what I expected. Bear with me, there was good and bad to this. Things that worked and things that didn't...<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1391106540i/8331999.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">"This should be interesting. If you're right, then what you're about to tell me is the secret to success for the average married man. I'd hate to miss a single word."<br></b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br>This book was nothing like the typical romance books we read. Don't go into it expecting a romance. For starters, it commits the cardinal sin as far as I am concerned, when it comes to love stories. It doesn't have a happy ending. It's left open to interpretation, it leaves you wondering, it leaves you with a million and one questions.<br><br>It does, however, have a leading lady, a good touch of steamy chemistry between our interviewer and our interviewee and a confession of love. Did I believe the 'love' between the two characters? Did I hell! It came from left field and just did nothing whatsoever to move me.<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1391106540i/8331999.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">"I need you, but I don't want you to fall in love with me."<br>"What makes you so sure that I will?"<br>I smiled, but there was no humour. "Because I'm fighting with all my strength to stop falling in love with you."<br></b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br>Secondly and leading on from me being unmoved, this whole thing was far, <i>far</i> too clinical for me. This book is exactly as the title suggests. It is an interview, conducted by a pretty young journalist, named Letitia, with renowned BDSM master, Jonah Noble. If you've read Ella Frank's <i>Bling Obsession</i>, there were parts of this that really reminded me of that, but nowhere near as emotive.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1392298391i/8534630._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Throughout the story, Jonah recounts his experiences with various lovers throughout his years as a dominant. That just didn't work for me. I didn't feel any connection to the characters and the second hand nature in which we learn about Jonah's previous partners just left me feeling a sense of detachment that I couldn't shake.<br><br>Did it turn me on? No, not really. It kind of just proves one of the things that Jonah states in the book... women do need an emotional connection to get the most out of sex. I felt no emotion for these characters at all and therefore read the scenes more like they were a sex-ed lesson, rather than a raunchy novel and characters that I could fall in love with. <br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1391106540i/8331999.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">"Women need to feel loved in order to want sex. And men need sex, in order to feel loved."</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br>However, it <i>did</i> intrigue me. Let's face it, thanks to <i>Fifty Shades</i> there has been a lot of speculation, a lot of fascination and a lot of rumour around the BDSM lifestyle. I'm sure some of the accounts we read are pretty accurate and some less so. So I was very interested to read from the POV of a 'BDSM Master' himself. <br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1391106540i/8331999.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">"She started to plead."<br>I looked at Leticia. "That was the real power," I said soflty. "That was what turned me on, and catapulted me into the world of BDSM. I loved the way Claire pleaded and begged for her release. It wasn't about physical domination for me. It still isn't. It's about that emotional transfer of power: the command and control. That's what turns me on, Leticia. That's what I find so addictive about being a Master. I love the power, given to me by the submissive. It's symbolic of their trust. Claire showed me how intoxicating that feeling could be."<br></b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br>Firstly, I wanted to hear things from a man's side and secondly I wanted to see how accurate the lovely Fifty and friends have been. I have to say, I didn't learn quite as much as I thought I might. In fact, some of it was a bit disappointing, to be honest. No red-room, no crazy music to accompany a mandatory flogging... Apparently things aren't really as crazy and intense as good ol' Christian and his Dom pals make out. Bummer. Of course, Jonah/Jason does state that ever BDSM relationship is different, but still... *pouts*<br><br>Now, where I felt this book really came into it's own was the way Jonah Noble understands what women want. <i>This</i> is what I think this book needs shouting from the rooftops about. Ladies, you all need to grab a copy of this book, shove it into your man's hands and force him to read it! You. Are. Welcome!<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1391106540i/8331999.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">"Leticia, no woman tastes like honey - but every man should tell the woman he is with that she does."<br>"What does that mean?"<br>"It means that every woman I have ever known intimately has been inhibited and self-concious about the way their pussy might taste to a man."<br>"Why?" <br>I shrugged. "How the hell would I know? You tell me. All I know is that women relax and let themselves go sexually once a man reassures her that he loves the way she tastes. I tell women they taste like honey."<br></b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br>Mr. Noble knows how to please his ladies. He's clearly spent years studying women and their reactions to every touch, every sound, every stimulant and he has taken notes. The man has done his homework. There are so many little tips and paragraphs in here that I was reading and thinking <i>'YES!! That is SO right! Every man needs to read this!'</i> In fact, I'm thinking of writing to whoever is in charge of marriages and suggesting they make reading <i>Interview with a Master</i> a stipulation for all husbands-to-be! I'm pretty sure divorce rates would plummet and ladies of the world would walk around with bigger smiles on their faces!<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1391106540i/8331999.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">"Every woman who is aroused by submission is also aroused by an alpha male who can tame her. These women aren't looking for a husband in the bedroom who will make them feel safe and loved. They already have that in their relationship. These women are looking for a man who is strong enough to conquer them. That way the woman can still feel vibrant and independent... but also feel comfortable submitting to their lover. That's the turn-on for women. They don't want to submissives... they want to feel like they can't resist submitting."</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br>And I don't mean that every couple should start involving BDSM in their bedroom antics. Jonah just outlines simple observations that can be applied to every day, ordinary, vanilla relationships. He touches on the wants and needs of both men and women and how they need to understand one another better. It's insightful.<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1391106540i/8331999.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">"I think women want men to be more like men again."<br></b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1392298391i/8534631.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>But then, there were also things from a man's POV that I just did not want to know. I didn't want to know that even when a man says 'I can't wait another second to have you' or is all overcome with need for his girl, that actually, it's all bull and he is just <i>acting</i> all overcome with need, when infact, he'd be quite capable of going and making a sandwich first. Yeh, I didn't wanna know that. I'd rather live in my little fantasy world where men just can't get enough of their women, thanks Jonah! Lol! I wanted to put my fingers in my ears and shout 'la la la la!'<br><br>So, I do think this book needed to be written. I'm glad Jason Luke put himself out there and told us how things are from a guys POV, and from the POV of a real life Dom.<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1391106540i/8331999.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">"Anticipation is more potent than a whip and more compelling than handcuffs. The ability to tease and arouse a woman is a subtly skill few men ever bother to learn," I said. "But learning the art of anticipation can make a woman go weak at the knees with longing."<br></b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br>And unfortunately for me, the anticipation really was everything. I found this book to be more of an educational sexual self-help book, than a romance novel I could lose myself in.<br><br><b>Have you read it? Tell us what you thought?</b><br><br><br><b><i>'Interview with a Master</i> Statistics</b><br><b>• Steam Rating (out of 5):</b> ♥♥♥♥♥<br><b>• Ending:</b> No HEA<br><b>• Length:</b> 258 pages<br><b>• Narrative:</b> Jonah's POV. First person. Past tense.<br><b>• Series:</b> ✗ <br><b>• Can this be read as a standalone?</b> Yes<br><b>• Themes:</b><br>BDSM<br>Male POV<br><b>• WARNING. This book includes...</b> <br>Graphic sexual content. BDSM scenes. <br><b>• Writing:</b> Good<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1389786435i/8054383._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><a href="http://smittensbookblog.wordpress.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1390158123i/8153947._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br><a href="http://www.amazon.co.uk/Interview-Master-Jason-Luke-ebook/dp/B00IB32RZY/ref=sr_1_1?ie=UTF8&amp;qid=1392296950&amp;sr=8-1&amp;keywords=interview+with+a+master" rel="nofollow noopener">

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Kim" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Kim" href="/user/show/11692522-kim">Kim</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>
