        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer836164734" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16702446835224757240">I was given an ARC of this book in exchange for an honest review, so here goes. Oh My God, Holy Cow and just Wow, Wow, Wow! Jason Luke has written a book similar to the style of Interview with a Vampire, and loosely based on his own life experiences in BDSM. We get to relive events from Master Jonah Noble’s life, while he speaks to his interviewer. Leticia is a young journalist trying to make a name for herself and decides to seek out Jonah for an interview. Jonah has a reputation for being a ha</span>
  <span id="freeText16702446835224757240" style="display:none">I was given an ARC of this book in exchange for an honest review, so here goes. Oh My God, Holy Cow and just Wow, Wow, Wow! Jason Luke has written a book similar to the style of Interview with a Vampire, and loosely based on his own life experiences in BDSM. We get to relive events from Master Jonah Noble’s life, while he speaks to his interviewer. Leticia is a young journalist trying to make a name for herself and decides to seek out Jonah for an interview. Jonah has a reputation for being a hard man to be with, he is of course gorgeous, strong, commanding and his eyes can bore into your soul, rendering you helpless to say no to him. As Leticia questions Jonah, listening to him reflect on his past, telling her stories of his life (in great detail I might add) on how he became the man he is today. Learning about Jonah’s life and what he endured as a teenager and everything else that led him to becoming a Master, had enabled them to gradually become friends. Leticia is secretly becoming attracted to Jonah, meeting with Jonah day after day is becoming more difficult for her to resist his charm, his strength. I found myself hoping they would start a relationship but Jonah is reluctant to give into his own feelings for Leticia. Jonah only has women in his life for his pleasure and hers, he has never had or wanted a loving relationship. Jonah plays the scene, Jonah demands his women are only in his life for the sex, the training of his Subs, and then he moves on. So does he give in and seduce Leticia? You will just have to read the book to find out. You won't regret it!<br /> Before I give away too much more I just have to say that I have read my share of BDSM books, but Jonah/Jason Luke is a genius! The things he says about women and men and marriage are really so true, I related to so many things that were discussed in this book. This world needs more men like Jonah, and I’m not just talking about a man that will spank and tie up his woman, (although that may be fun) I am talking about a man that will take the time to truly understand a woman and expect her to do the same, to have a mutual relationship of respect and trust. BDSM is not about controlling a woman and satisfying the man, it’s about ‘do ut des’ “I give that you may give”, that quote has so much meaning and I get it now. I will and have recommended this book to all my friends that like to read. I give this book 5 out of 5 stars and will probably read this one several times. I am hopeful that we will hear more about Jonah and Leticia, I really do! Just start writing that book now Jason cause this book is going to break records. Move over Christian Grey cause Jonah Noble is here.<br /><br />5 out of 5 stars from The Book Nut ~ Kim<br /><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.facebook.com/TheBookNuts">www.facebook.com/TheBookNuts</a><br /><br /><br /></span>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/849158987?book_show_action=true">Feb 08, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer849158987" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7723089187279316022">Jason Luke, Interview with a Master. Frank.Controlled,Well Executed. <br/><br/>I deliberately didn't read this book right out of the block, because there was a lot of publicity surrounding it. Not because I didn't want to read it, but because I didn't want my judgement to be swayed by all the positive buzz surrounding it. (I did bump it up my reading list though, because it is one of my favourite genres.) So with these points in mind... <br/><br/>The main character,Jonah Noble, (The Master) is a very well developed</span>
  <span id="freeText7723089187279316022" style="display:none">Jason Luke, Interview with a Master. Frank.Controlled,Well Executed. <br /><br />I deliberately didn't read this book right out of the block, because there was a lot of publicity surrounding it. Not because I didn't want to read it, but because I didn't want my judgement to be swayed by all the positive buzz surrounding it. (I did bump it up my reading list though, because it is one of my favourite genres.) So with these points in mind... <br /><br />The main character,Jonah Noble, (The Master) is a very well developed character, and one has an immediate 'feel' for his cool,controlled and commanding persona. Jonah's honest account and frankly delivered monologues and dialogue he has, with the female character Leticia.are enticing.( love the names by the way.) <br /><br />The book evokes a range of feelings for me as a reader. This man is definitely 'in tune' with how the mind of a woman works. The character demonstrates this at various points with his explanations of aspects of BDSM and how the relationships between A Dominant and Submissive are derived. His careful observations of Leticia both in how she is perceiving her role in the interview and as a woman are excellently penned. I had a sense on one hand; of affection, attraction and admiration by Jonah for Leticia. These affectionate feelings were contradicted at times by the honed techniques of Jonah the Master. By nature, Jonah the Master constantly assesses and reassess Leticia, with calculating questions and his personal observations. Jason Luke created the 'anticipation factor' which touched me emotionally keeping me 'off balance' with the expectation that something may happen at any moment. He demonstrated, controlled poise,slow dialogue and carefully chosen words, which allowed the reader to be lead through the interview, disclosing Jonah's thoughts and spoken words, which complimented the story line excellently. I am looking forward to Book two in the future. A first book for Jason Luke, but definitely not the last, keep them coming.</span>

          </span>

  <span id="freeText11561132202251328939" style="display:none">5 glistening, Big Book of Rules stars...<br /><br />What a fantastic, unique, compulsive story!<br /><br />I didn't know quite what to expect when I impatiently picked up Interview With a Master on release day, but I knew, given the tantalising hype, that it was a "must read right now" for me.<br /><br />The premise of the book is as the title suggests; the elusive, notorious BDSM Master, Jonah Noble, is to be interviewed by a young intern, Leticia Fall. <br /><br />Told entirely from Jonah's POV, we are guided through the story of how Jonah reached his notoriety. The interactions between Leticia and himself form a major part of the dialogue, interspersed with pauses in the story to focus on Leticia.<br /><br /><b>
  <blockquote>"Do ut des-I give that you may give"</blockquote>
</b><br /><br />As Jonah relays his past, he is also trying to convey the meaning, for him, of the BDSM lifestyle he has led. Leticia is intrigued and glued to his every word, completing many notebooks scribbled with this incomparable tale.<br /><br />The chemistry between the two characters is breathtaking, and is what I felt made the story a 5 star read for me.<br /><br />I don't really want to say any more about the storyline, because it is unique and a most wondrous experience. I would urge you to take the plunge, and hope that it captures you in the same way. I would very much like to see if this story can be continued...please Sir!<br /><br /><b>
  <blockquote>"It's not all about charming doms and beautiful breathless subs."</blockquote>

  <span id="freeText5883611666534071615" style="display:none">This book did not sit right with me at all. <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1393262826ra/8684190.gif" width="396" height="170" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>and because of how badly some fans are reacting to reviews, I wasn't even going to give my opinion on it<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1393260915ra/8684044.gif" width="400" height="246" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>but I decided <s> that it was important to have as many differing opinions so that people can make an informed judgement about whether or not they should read this book.</s> Ah, screw 'em.<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1393312947ra/8692657.gif" width="400" height="243" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br> So here goes. <br>The story is told mainly in flashbacks as the "Master" Jonah Noble tells his story to journalist Leticia. He tells Leticia all about his sexual conquests supposedly in explicit detail, and yet this was the most boring erotica I have ever read.<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1393268605ra/8684983.gif" width="245" height="214" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>I felt like I was reading a badly written self help book. We do gleam some facts about the BDSM lifestyle but they are so rudimentary that you could learn everything he says from a Google search. Also his actions and views about women seem to counter what he tells Leticia about being a Master. I found Nobel to be chauvinistic and conceited.<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1393358202ra/8700104.gif" width="400" height="261" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br> He seems to think that an interview with him will make her career. Why? Because he was a "Master"? Because he was rich? She could have interviewed any Master and got similar results, and I got tired pretty quick of him thinking he knew what woman wanted and how "real" men act. At one point he describes a woman's breasts as pubescent...seriously? that's the word choice you're going with? Then there was this gem <br><br>"Women have three defenses they use against a man to get their way," I said. "The first defense is tears. The second defense is abuse, and the third defense is violence..."<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1393352185ra/8699090.gif" width="400" height="281" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br>Leticia wasn't much better. She came across as an unrealistic, simpering child. She does no research into BDSM and then has to be told by Nobel how to be a journalist. She tells him about a one night stand she had then worries he'll think she's a slut. Uh, hello? man whore telling you about all the women he's slept with. Then when they do kiss he pushes her away, cause you know Masters don't fall in love, and worries that it's her fault cause she didn't kiss him right. At the end she has a total melt down because she thinks he's cheated on her in this imaginary relationship they have together.<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1393357067ra/8699968.gif" width="400" height="232" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>They never actually have sex by the way. Maybe I'm unique, but I'm pretty ambidextrous at getting myself off. <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1393358500ra/8700124.gif" width="400" height="281" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br>The only thing I found slightly interesting was Noble's Silence of the Lambs-esque "Do ut des". All in all I thought the characters were cliched, one dimensional, and just all around unlikable that I wasn't able to connect to either of them. This book is way too over hyped for what you get, and it seems to be all gimmick and marketing. Say it's written by a man from a man's point of view and<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1393356924ra/8699950.gif" width="400" height="212" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br>I'm not sure why that is but I hope other male writers in this genre don't take pointers from Jason Luke. If you read this book and liked it more power to you. We should all read what we enjoy but I hope that you also read some of the other BDSM erotica out there <br><br><br><br><br><br><br><br><br><br><br><br><br><br><br><br><br><br></span>

  <span id="freeText15837237612742576824" style="display:none">This is sad. I understand parts of this book are autobiographical. I sure hope it's not the part for the reason he did not allow anyone to get close.  I was really wanting to feel like I was inside the head of a Dom. If I was, he has to be the most vanilla Dom I have run across. The stories he decides to relate to a reporter regarding the story of his life were ridiculous. I know the author meant them to be hot but I felt like each story was fake and censored and nowhere near even lukewarm. It left me, as the reader, disconnected and empty.. <br /><br />If there is a woman around that even comes close to being as naive and just flat ignorant as this female reporter, she couldn't be older than 13. THIS is the reason I stopped reading most FM books and switched to MM. Surely I'm not so jaded to believe that someone in their mid-twenties is actually not that stupid. Do men actually find stupid women attractive? So, you won't find any connection with the female character in this book either. <br /><br />Here Is the sad part. This author has the potential to be a good author. He just didn't have the proverbial balls to actually come up with the goods. I feel as if anything close to being the truth was censored. In my mind I see him with pen in hand, it shakes while he ponders what he wants to says and then his shoulders slump in defeat as he gives into his fear. I hope he takes all of the criticism and writes again with some guts. </span>

<span id="freeTextContainer3409305678058946199">I just finished Interview with a Master and I am left disappointed. I was going to wait until tomorrow to write my review. But decided I was not going to sleep on it. And it's my first review ever on goodreads so here I go:<br/><br/>I give one star for the steamy scenes and second star for it being different. <br/><br/>I understand that it was an "interview" but it lacked a story line.   <span id="freeText3409305678058946199" style="display:none">I just finished Interview with a Master and I am left disappointed. I was going to wait until tomorrow to write my review. But decided I was not going to sleep on it. And it's my first review ever on goodreads so here I go:<br /><br />I give one star for the steamy scenes and second star for it being different. <br /><br />I understand that it was an "interview" but it lacked a story line. It was about Jonah and his sexual encounters. 3 women at different times in his life. What confuses me was why he felt compelled to tell his story to an amateur reporter? Really?!? He owned publishing companies and could have found someone more suitable. <br /><br />I didn't care to read about Letitia's family history and the ex boyfriend. She wasn't likable in my eyes. Leticia annoyed me as she was incredibly naive. "Did you like it when you did "----" to the submissive?" Made it for a eye-rolling read. And what was up with her reaction at the end? I don't want to give any spoilers but her character flip out was bizarre, it didn't make sense. <br /><br />The best analogy for this books is the Magic Mike movie. Great visuals but lack of a storyline. The sex scenes were hot yet seemed so distant. <br /><br />The ending left me with a sour look, contemplating reading the 2nd book. Perhaps my curiosity will get the best of me. </span>

</a><br/><br/>Jonah is a Master, a Dominate and an alpha male. He has had over a decade of experience in the BDSM life style and he’s sharing his past experiences. Leticia is the journalist that gets to interview him.<br/><br/>I so wanted to read this book because I heard the author shared real-life experiences. Sounds very intriguing right? As a debut author, I give Interview with a Master an okay and great attempt, but there are some things th</span>
  <span id="freeText18245449919967526253" style="display:none"> <b>3.5 Seductive Scandalous Stars</b><br><br><b>The key to the best sex is anticipation…</b><br><br><a href="http://imgur.com/pzEfAlz" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1392083156ra/8497683.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Jonah is a Master, a Dominate and an alpha male. He has had over a decade of experience in the BDSM life style and he’s sharing his past experiences. Leticia is the journalist that gets to interview him.<br><br>I so wanted to read this book because I heard the author shared real-life experiences. Sounds very intriguing right? As a debut author, I give Interview with a Master an okay and great attempt, but there are some things that just fell flat for me and didn’t work out.<br><br>I love the plot and since it’s about the Hero telling stories, I didn’t expect a super romantic story, what I was expecting was something very kinky and fun. I think I had too high of expectations.<br><br>Throughout the book Leticia and Jonah meet at each other’s places for the interview. The interview is conducted over several days and sometimes they meet more than once a day. Jonah doesn’t talk about his life in detail, but just shares a few past experiences, three ladies to be exact. As he describes each lady, he goes into detail about his sexual encounters.<br><br>First off, I love that it’s a story telling book, I think if there were flash backs, I wouldn’t have built a relationship with Jonah and Leticia. Every once in a while the dialogue is interrupted by a scene transition or change of subject. Jonah will only continue with the interview if he can ask Leticia personal questions, like when was the last time she orgasm. So there’s an underlying romance there, very tiny, but it’s noticeable. <br><br>The main flaw of the book is how short the read is. It’s too short to build any kind of chemistry between Jonah and Leticia. I kind of wanted like months of interviews, maybe she’s writing a book instead. Also, the other thing I have a problem with is how soft the BDSM is. I’m a hardcore BDSM reader and I’m pretty much open to all forms of play, so I have little patience in someone explaining to me what soft limit and safe word is. I just wanted crazy kink you know? <br><br>I am not sure if I want to move on with the series. On one hand the ending kind of disappointed me because it was just so random, but then the overall plot and idea is interesting. I think the kink needs to be amp up a notch and there needs to be more development of characters for me to move forward. The steam is there, but it’s just so light and fluffy despite the dark theme.<br><br>Interview with a Master is unique and different read that didn’t hit all marks, but was enjoyable to read regardless. <br><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/20569957.Interview_with_a_Master__Interview_with_a_Master___1_" title="Interview with a Master (Interview with a Master, #1) by Jason Luke" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1390052489s/20569957.jpg" alt="Interview with a Master (Interview with a Master, #1) by Jason Luke" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <a href="http://www.amazon.com/gp/product/B00IB32RZY/ref=as_li_qf_sp_asin_tl?ie=UTF8&amp;camp=211189&amp;creative=373489&amp;creativeASIN=B00IB32RZY&amp;link_code=as3&amp;tag=jacqsread-20" rel="nofollow noopener">AMAZON</a></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer8225116310986313584"><i>Holy crap. Holy crap. Holy crap.</i>... That's my reaction after reading this AMAZING book by <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/7776521.Jason_Luke' title='Jason Luke' rel='nofollow noopener'>Jason Luke</a><br/><br/><i>
  <blockquote>
    <b>"Husbands and lovers need to make the woman in their life feel conquered" -Jonah Noble</b>
  </blockquote>
</i> <br/><br/>This entire novel is set up with freelance journalist <b>Leticia</b> interviewing BDSM Master <b>Jonah Noble</b> about his lifestyle. We don't know why he's set up this interview on his very personal life, nor do we know much about him. It's what he reveals in the interview that transforms our opinion of the BDSM </span>
  <span id="freeText8225116310986313584" style="display:none"><i>Holy crap. Holy crap. Holy crap.</i>... That's my reaction after reading this AMAZING book by <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/7776521.Jason_Luke" title="Jason Luke" rel="nofollow noopener">Jason Luke</a><br /><br /><i>
  <blockquote>
    <b>"Husbands and lovers need to make the woman in their life feel conquered" -Jonah Noble</b>
  </blockquote>
</i> <br /><br />This entire novel is set up with freelance journalist <b>Leticia</b> interviewing BDSM Master <b>Jonah Noble</b> about his lifestyle. We don't know why he's set up this interview on his very personal life, nor do we know much about him. It's what he reveals in the interview that transforms our opinion of the BDSM lifestyle and our opinions of Jonah.<br /><br /><i>
  <blockquote>
    <b>" 'Over the months that followed we learned about the lifestyle together. I guess you would call it "on-the-job" training.' I smiled to myself. I liked that line. I'd have to remember it." -Jonah Noble</b>
  </blockquote>
</i> <br /><br />Jonah is a gosh darn mystery that every woman wants to explore. This is one of the best books I've ever read. It's coming to us from a man who isn't an expert on the topic but someone who has encountered it in their lifetime. I don't think I've ever read anything that has summed up what women want from a relationship and a BDSM one at that. <br /><br /><i>
  <blockquote>
    <b>"Every woman who is aroused by submission is also aroused by an alpha male who can tame her. These women aren’t looking for a husband in the bedroom who will make them feel safe and loved. [...] These women are looking for a man who is strong enough to conquer them. That way the woman can still feel vibrant and independent… but also feel comfortable submitting to their lover. That’s the turn-on for women. They don’t want to be submissives… they want to feel like they can’t resist submitting." -Jonah Noble</b>
  </blockquote>
</i> <br /><br />I think what I really loved about this book was that not only is the reader getting a behind the scenes of Jonah's past, but we witnessed to romance between Leticia and Jonah.<br /><br />Overall, I think this is going to be a powerful book for relationships. Couples need to read these books to understand the dynamic of what they could pursue together. I'm giving this read <b>5 STARS out of 5 STARS</b> because this book is an example of genius literature. This is what women and men should be reading.<br /><br /><i>Fingers crossed there will be a second book... please!!</i><br /><br />~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~<br />Read by Taryn Lee on February 8, 2014<br />Reviewed by Taryn Lee on February 8, 2014<br /><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://facebook.com/tarynleesblog">http://facebook.com/tarynleesblog</a></span>

<div id="review_835134463" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/835134463" />
    <a title="Claire Robinson" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/14026987-claire-robinson"><img alt="Claire Robinson" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1431471072p2/14026987.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/835134463?book_show_action=true">Jan 26, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Claire Robinson" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Claire Robinson" href="/user/show/14026987-claire-robinson">Claire Robinson</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer835134463" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2169111347379903540">4 Stars.<br/><br/> “The Jonah Noble Big Book Of Rules” certainly contains quite a few pearls of wisdom, they are all enlightening in their own way, and extremely well thought out.<br/><br/><b>BDSM is about two people, trying to discover what makes them happy in life – what gives them a sense of belonging and completion.</b><br/><br/>Interview with a Master is a work of fiction based a little on fact, that features BDSM. I wouldn’t say it is a book about BDSM in the traditional sense. You will understand what I mean when you read it</span>
  <span id="freeText2169111347379903540" style="display:none">4 Stars.<br /><br /> “The Jonah Noble Big Book Of Rules” certainly contains quite a few pearls of wisdom, they are all enlightening in their own way, and extremely well thought out.<br /><br /><b>BDSM is about two people, trying to discover what makes them happy in life – what gives them a sense of belonging and completion.</b><br /><br />Interview with a Master is a work of fiction based a little on fact, that features BDSM. I wouldn’t say it is a book about BDSM in the traditional sense. You will understand what I mean when you read it. I will say that in reading the book and being able to appreciate it fully you will firstly need to forget everything you have ever read before about the subject (I did anyway), and go into it with an open mind. <br /><br /><b>Jonah – “BDSM isn’t the solution to every relationship in trouble, it’s not the answer for every lonely girl looking for love, and it’s not about charming doms and beautiful breathless subs.”</b><br /><br />You will not find massive long paragraphs of inner monologue, or lots of swinging from one emotional minefield to the next, there are no inner goddesses or red rooms of pain. This is a book about a man, written by a man, and the language and writing style highlight these things beautifully. It is a pretty frank, and at points quite blunt and very on point monologue, but that is what makes it so special. Flowery language and overly descriptive text would not have worked for this book, Jonah Noble is a pretty eloquent and candid, get to the point kind of guy, and Jason Luke has used language that portrays him perfectly that way. What makes it even more appealing though are the moments of sheer comedy that he has managed to thread into the story…<br /><br /><b>Jonah – “The BDSM lifestyle is like…seafood,”…”And seafood comes in a hundred different forms”.</b><br /><br />I never thought I would see BDSM and seafood used in the same sentence together!<br /><br />But for all of the straightforwardness of the writing Jason Luke has also managed to add a lot of beautifully put together paragraphs, the language used is vital and offers total clarity as to what Jonah is trying to impart to Leticia for the writing of her article. <br /><br /><b>Leticia – “Define Sexy.”<br /><br />Jonah – “I don’t have a definition, not do I have specific parameters. It is not any one thing about a woman that makes her sexy in my eyes; it’s a collection of things – an intoxicating fusion of the obvious and the subtle that merge together.”</b><br /><br />What begins as a series of interviews between an intern looking to become a fully fledged reporter and a known Master, develops as the time they spend together increases, and I found myself holding my breath at points waiting to see what would happen next or where Jason would take the story. <br /><br /><b>I narrowed my eyes and came up out of the chair with slow menace. I prowled across the room, drawing out the silence, moving in the dull gloom like I was hunting prey.</b><br /><br />But this is on no way your standard boy meets girl or man meets woman tale. It is more, it is deeper and the relationship feels more realistic because of it. The only thing I am totally bummed about…. the fact I need more of Jonah Noble and his unforgettable charm in my life. We are left at a bit of a cliffhanger, and I really would love to see where Jason intends on taking Jonah and Leticia’s tale next, there is certainly a whole wealth of options in my opinion.<br /><br />I wouldn’t define this book as BDSM Erotica, it is broader than that and to be honest if you enjoy a good story, with well written characters, some sexy times and a bit of humor thrown in, I don’t think you will go wrong with Interview with a Master.<br /><br />ARC kindly provided by the author in exchange for the above honest review. I look forward to reading whatever Mr. Luke has in store for us in the future as this is a pretty special debut in my humble opinion!<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="2169111347379903540" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15389709-marissa-honeycutt?shelf=erotica">erotica</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer836335682" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10092947285690711422">Wow. <br/><br/>I waited for hours after Jason posted that he had 'pushed the button' for it to be released with dozens of other anticipating fans on Facebook. We had a great time, speculating, gossiping, building (I think) friendships. And then I got the email. I literally squealed, making my 7-year-old ask why I just squeaked like a mouse. :)<br/><br/>So, I started reading it. And it was awesome. And then, about 2/3 of the way through, I started getting depressed. I was mentally blogging about how the book was mak</span>
  <span id="freeText10092947285690711422" style="display:none">Wow. <br /><br />I waited for hours after Jason posted that he had 'pushed the button' for it to be released with dozens of other anticipating fans on Facebook. We had a great time, speculating, gossiping, building (I think) friendships. And then I got the email. I literally squealed, making my 7-year-old ask why I just squeaked like a mouse. :)<br /><br />So, I started reading it. And it was awesome. And then, about 2/3 of the way through, I started getting depressed. I was mentally blogging about how the book was making me feel. Thinking it was a dangerous book to read because it made me long for something that I doubt would ever happen in real life. Yes, I know it's fiction, but there's that element of wanting a Master...And because of things I've done in my past, I don't know if I could ever be that 'type of woman.' A woman that would thrive under a Master, at least not in the way I would want to. (But that's a whole other story.) But that's not Jason's fault...that's all me, and, like I said, his book was amazing...fantastic...everything I hoped and more.<br /><br />Jonah Noble is everything that the ARC reviewers said he was. Everything the teasers my online friends made up. He was...amazing. Sexy, rough, arrogant (in a good way). And then there was the question that he wouldn't answer and it knocked my depression right out of me. I was literally stunned. I stared at my Kindle, hands shaking and disbelief flooding my brain. <br /><br />I don't cry. I hate crying. Hate! It! I avoid movies and books that make me cry. And tears ran down my cheeks as I read the last few pages of the book. Not a lot. I didn't bawl. I didn't sob. Just a few big, fat tears rolling down my cheeks. Even now, I'm shaking from the emotion that coursed through my body from the ending. <br /><br />I am completely...satisfied doesn't touch how I feel... Satiated is the word. I am completely satiated with this book; like after a great round of sex that touches your mind, soul and spirit. It was a fantastic, amazing, beautiful few hours that I spent getting to know Jonah Noble. <br /><br />This is so much more than a BDSM book. Jason/Jonah 'gets'...understands... women...at least, women like me. Everything he said, at least in my mind, is true. (I'm sending this over to my hubby's Kindle as soon as I finish writing this. lol.)<br /><br />What more can I say? My mind is still reeling from the ending...<br /><br />Wow.</span>

<div id="review_853591297" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/853591297" />
    <a title="Eveline" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/21314852-eveline"><img alt="Eveline" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1371241963p2/21314852.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/853591297?book_show_action=true">Feb 13, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Eveline" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Eveline" href="/user/show/21314852-eveline">Eveline</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer853591297" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15425597335066866436">This book made me angry. Seriously angry.<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1392292717ra/8533730.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>It started with the advertising -- hyped as bdsm written by a MAN. In capital letters. Listen, Mr. Luke, yes, erotica and romance is one of the very fields in fiction, in which there are more women writers then men. That is also why it is one of the most laughed about generally denigrated, just porn and fan fiction, and we who read it are treated like horny idiots who wouldn't know literature if it smacked us in the face.<br/>To come in and pretend you get pro</span>
  <span id="freeText15425597335066866436" style="display:none">This book made me angry. Seriously angry.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1392292717ra/8533730.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>It started with the advertising -- hyped as bdsm written by a MAN. In capital letters. Listen, Mr. Luke, yes, erotica and romance is one of the very fields in fiction, in which there are more women writers then men. That is also why it is one of the most laughed about generally denigrated, just porn and fan fiction, and we who read it are treated like horny idiots who wouldn't know literature if it smacked us in the face.<br>To come in and pretend you get props just for being a man, is one of the most insulting, patronizing ass-hattery I've ever heard.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1381128764ra/4305596.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Have you ever seen something like "Lit fic written by a WOMAN." or "Sci-Fi like you've never read it before -- written by a GIRL from a GIRL's point of view!" <br><br>Newflash: There are a lot of men in erotica, there are also a lot of books written from a male POV. Get off your high Mastery horse.<br><br>Now to the story. If you can call it that. I actually couldn't finish it, I got too angry at the constant man-splaining. What makes men think they get to teach me -- a woman -- about being a woman. They do try it every time, though. <br>In the end, this book is the same old trope of the stupid dominant, who uses bdsm as an outlet for his general disrespect of women (the way he describes Laetica makes that more than obvious). He touts the old tropes of "Falling in love is the worst mistake a master can make" -- um, nope. The worst mistake a Master can make is to believe that trope and I HATE the author for perpetuating this to people who may be curious about the lifestyle and look for guidance in books like this.<br>I was told bullshit like this for years, and I am so glad that after some good solid and loving bdsm relationships I know who i am and what I'm worth. And a "master" like this one... yeah, super turn-off.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1392292717ra/8533731.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1392292717ra/8533732.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br></span>
  <a data-text-id="15425597335066866436" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('Ke7D0iQXVfnkTCj4ajXEj2vrfhNLBj/5E+bFv/x0rw3y5J4vsRrI/wBQ577kaIDIvw8x+KdYDrTW+vIcJOadNA==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('tV/XFSxHAGjOiigIE7uPJ0V0kQvNhD0qJTcxtxET/3BuVYrouUqdbiqW506d5stgkZDe4CHaDGfgKwYUyYHNSQ==')})
  }

  <span id="freeText3659432227151360720" style="display:none">Jason Luke enjoyed several years involved in the BDSM lifestyle - but he is quick to point out that his experiences don't qualify him as an expert, any more than knowing how to drive a car makes him a qualified mechanic. 'Interview with a Master' is a novel about how one man became a Master. The book is a work of fiction, but Jason has drawn heavily on encounters from his own real life. He won't say which parts of the book are fictionalised, and which parts are auto-biographical.<br /><br />Erotic BDSM fiction written by a man from a man's point of view.</span>
